17/03/2023, 16:44 - Ravi Desai: ğŸ”´ Hello Folks, check out this YouTube channel. One of the best channel I found for Machine Learning and Data Science. He covers everything from maths, algorithms and end to end projects. Check out the playlist those who all are interested in this field. You won't be requiring any other course.
17/03/2023, 16:45 - Ravi Desai: Roadmap for ML/DS:
1. Start with Python: https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLKnIA16_Rmvb1RYR-iTA_hzckhdONtSW4

99% of time you'll be using python for almost everything. Whatever is covered in the playlist is more than sufficient. No need to for R or any other language. Learn about virtual environments and python package management. It'll be used while deploying your models.

2. NumPy, Pandas, Matplotlib, Seaborn: You'll find separate playlists for all these libraries in the channel. 

3. Learn basics of Statistics, Linear Algebra and EDA (Exploratory Data Analysis): https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLKnIA16_RmvZAqJzKstVHywcRNMn6pcGD
At this stage you can also learn analytics tools like Tableau, PowerBI and complete some analytics projects.

4. Time for MLDLC (Machine Learning Development Life Cycle) and Algorithms: https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLKnIA16_Rmvbr7zKYQuBfsVkjoLcJgxHH

Complete the playlist in the same order. He covers everything from basics till advance along with implementations of algorithms.

5. Move on to end to end projects: You can learn about flask, or django. If not you can use fastAPI, pickle, streamlit. Learn to containerize and deploy your models. 
https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLKnIA16_RmvY5eP91BGPa0vXUYmIdtfPQ

10/08/2023, 14:41 - Ravi Desai: *An advice from 4Y CC members regarding unpaid internships*

Hey @2025-batch
Just a word from 4th year coding club members,
We spotted a lot of people started working for unpaid roles at some organizations. (or even worse- you guys are paying them to get an internship)
You are in third year its high time to realize its merely a scam. It gives you a fake sense of achievement which in real world stands with 0 value. If you are really interested in getting experience there are tons of things to do, make a personal project, work in teams on some projects, learn from udemy, participate in hackathons, contribute to open source. These things will give you *an actual experience*, don't start working in any of those unpaid orgs. 
Again talk to people who have achieved something in their field, don't get trapped in such organizations on listening someone's naive advice

06/03/2024, 19:33 - à¸£Î±É±Î±É¾Æ­É¦: import pandas as pd
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns

# Load milk and egg production datasets
milk_data = pd.read_csv('/content/Milk_Production_2007_2012 (1).csv')
egg_data = pd.read_csv('/content/Egg_Production_2007_2012 (1).csv')

# Rename columns of the egg dataset for clarity
egg_data.columns = ['States/Uts', '2007-08', '2008-09', '2009-10', '2010-11', '2011-12']

# Merge the datasets on the 'States/Uts' column
merged_data = pd.merge(milk_data, egg_data, on='States/Uts', how='inner')

# Define the years for analysis
years = ['2007-08', '2008-09', '2009-10', '2010-11', '2011-12']

# Iterate over each year for visualization
for year in years:
    # Extract data for the current year
    year_data = merged_data[['States/Uts', year + '_x', year + '_y']]

    # Plot milk production for the current year
    plt.figure(figsize=(10, 6))
    sns.barplot(x='States/Uts', y=year+'_x', data=year_data)
    plt.title('Milk Production in ' + year)
    plt.xticks(rotation=90)
    plt.xlabel('States/Uts')
    plt.ylabel('Milk Production')
    plt.show()

    # Plot egg production for the current year
    plt.figure(figsize=(10, 6))
    sns.barplot(x='States/Uts', y=year+'_y', data=year_data)
    plt.title('Egg Production in ' + year)
    plt.xticks(rotation=90)
    plt.xlabel('States/Uts')
    plt.ylabel('Egg Production')
    plt.show()

    # Plot milk vs egg production for the current year
    plt.figure(figsize=(10, 6))
    sns.scatterplot(x=year + '_x', y= year + '_y', data=year_data, hue='States/Uts', legend='full')
    plt.title('Milk vs Egg Production in ' + year)
    plt.xlabel('Milk Production')
    plt.ylabel('Egg Production')
    plt.show()
